.keel/epics/VFDv1i61H/voyages/VFDv3gE5m/RECURSIVE_PLANNER_PROOF.md --- Text
 1 # Recursive Planner Proof
 2 
 3 ## Implemented Backbone
 4 
 5 - Interpretation-time operator memory now includes `AGENTS.md` plus linked foundational guidance excerpts in [agent_memory.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/agent_memory.rs).
 6 - The recursive planner contract lives in [planning.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/domain/ports/planning.rs) and is rendered through typed turn events in [turns.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/domain/model/turns.rs).
 7 - The application now routes non-trivial turns through a planner-owned loop in [mod.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/application/mod.rs), with bounded `search`, `read`, `inspect`, `refine`, `branch`, and `stop` actions.
 8 - Planner and synthesizer roles are independently configurable through [main.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/main.rs) and [mod.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/application/mod.rs), with the planner adapter wired in [sift_planner.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/sift_planner.rs) and planner action selection implemented in [sift_agent.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/sift_agent.rs).
 9 - The default transcript UI now renders interpretation context, planner capability, planner actions, and planner summaries in [interactive_tui.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/cli/interactive_tui.rs).
10 
11 ## Documentation Sync
12 
13 - The recursive harness backbone, current runtime lanes, and planner/synth split were updated in [README.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/README.md).
14 - The detailed implementation snapshot was updated in [ARCHITECTURE.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/ARCHITECTURE.md).
15 - Operational invariants and operator guidance were updated in [POLICY.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/POLICY.md), [AGENTS.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/AGENTS.md), [INSTRUCTIONS.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/INSTRUCTIONS.md), and [CONFIGURATION.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/CONFIGURATION.md).

2546 ... 263 fn discover_linked_documents(agent_path: &Path, contents: &str) -> Vec<PathBuf> {
2547 ... 264     let mut ordered = Vec::new();
2548 ... 265     let mut seen = HashSet::new();
2549 ... 266     for target in extract_markdown_link_targets(contents)
2550 ... 267         .into_iter()
2551 ... 268         .chain(extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents))
2552 ... 269     {
2553 ... 270         let Some(resolved) = resolve_link_target(agent_path, &target) else {
2554 ... 271             continue;
2555 ... 272         };
2556 ... 273         let canonical = canonical_memory_path(&resolved);
2557 ... 274         if seen.insert(canonical) {
2558 ... 275             ordered.push(resolved);
2559 ... 276         }
2560 ... 277     }
2561 ... 278     ordered
2562 ... 279 }
2563 ... 280 
2564 ... 281 fn extract_markdown_link_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2565 ... 282     let mut targets = Vec::new();
2566 ... 283     let mut remainder = contents;
2567 ... 284     while let Some(start) = remainder.find("](") {
2568 ... 285         let candidate = &remainder[start + 2..];
2569 ... 286         let Some(end) = candidate.find(')') else {
2570 ... 287             break;
2571 ... 288         };
2572 ... 289         let target = candidate[..end].trim();
2573 ... 290         if !target.is_empty() {
2574 ... 291             targets.push(target.to_string());
2575 ... 292         }
2576 ... 293         remainder = &candidate[end + 1..];
2577 ... 294     }
2578 ... 295     targets
2579 ... 296 }
2580 ... 297 
2581 ... 298 fn extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2582 ... 299     let mut targets = Vec::new();
2583 ... 300     let mut in_tick = false;
2584 ... 301     let mut current = String::new();
2585 ... 302 
2586 ... 303     for ch in contents.chars() {
2587 ... 304         if ch == '`' {
2588 ... 305             if in_tick {
2589 ... 306                 let trimmed = current.trim();
2590 ... 307                 if looks_like_local_doc_target(trimmed) {
2591 ... 308                     targets.push(trimmed.to_string());
2592 ... 309                 }
2593 ... 310                 current.clear();
2594 ... 311             }
2595 ... 312             in_tick = !in_tick;
2596 ... 313             continue;
2597 ... 314         }
2598 ... 315 
2599 ... 316         if in_tick {
2600 ... 317             current.push(ch);
2601 ... 318         }
2602 ... 319     }
2603 ... 320 
2604 ... 321     targets
2605 ... 322 }
2606 ... 323 
2607 ... 324 fn looks_like_local_doc_target(target: &str) -> bool {
2608 ... 325     target.ends_with(".md") || target.starts_with(".keel/")
2609 ... 326 }
2610 ... 327 
2611 ... 328 fn resolve_link_target(agent_path: &Path, target: &str) -> Option<PathBuf> {
2612 ... 329     if target.starts_with("http://")
2613 ... 330         || target.starts_with("https://")
2614 ... 331         || target.starts_with("mailto:")
2615 ... 332     {
2616 ... 333         return None;
2617 ... 334     }
2618 ... 335 
2619 ... 336     let target = target.split('#').next()?.trim();
2620 ... 337     if target.is_empty() || !looks_like_local_doc_target(target) {
2621 ... 338         return None;
2622 ... 339     }
2623 ... 340 
2624 ... 341     let candidate = if Path::new(target).is_absolute() {
2625 ... 342         PathBuf::from(target)
2626 ... 343     } else {
2627 ... 344         agent_path.parent()?.join(target)
2628 ... 345     };
2629 ... 346 
2630 ... 347     if candidate.is_file() {
2631 ... 348         Some(candidate)
2632 ... 349     } else {
2633 ... 350         None
2634 ... 351     }
2635 ... 352 }

2651 ... 374 fn select_relevant_excerpt(contents: &str, user_prompt: &str) -> (String, usize) {
2652 ... 375     let query_terms = prompt_terms(user_prompt);
2653 ... 376     let lines = contents.lines().collect::<Vec<_>>();
2654 ... 377 
2655 ... 378     let mut excerpt = Vec::new();
2656 ... 379     let mut score = 0;
2657 ... 380     if !query_terms.is_empty() {
2658 ... 381         for (index, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {
2659 ... 382             let normalized = line.to_ascii_lowercase();
2660 ... 383             let matched_terms = query_terms
2661 ... 384                 .iter()
2662 ... 385                 .filter(|term| normalized.contains(term.as_str()))
2663 ... 386                 .count();
2664 ... 387             if matched_terms > 0 {
2665 ... 388                 score += matched_terms;
2666 ... 389                 let start = index.saturating_sub(1);
2667 ... 390                 let end = usize::min(index + 3, lines.len());
2668 ... 391                 excerpt.extend(lines[start..end].iter().copied());
2669 ... 392                 if excerpt.len() >= 8 {
2670 ... 393                     break;
2671 ... 394                 }
2672 ... 395             }
2673 ... 396         }
2674 ... 397     }
2675 ... 398 
2676 ... 399     if excerpt.is_empty() {
2677 ... 400         excerpt.extend(
2678 ... 401             lines
2679 ... 402                 .into_iter()
2680 ... 403                 .filter(|line| !line.trim().is_empty())
2681 ... 404                 .take(8),
2682 ... 405         );
2683 ... 406     }
2684 ... 407 
2685 ... 408     (trim_memory_contents(&excerpt.join("\n")), score)
2686 ... 409 }
2687 ... 410 
2688 ... 411 fn prompt_terms(user_prompt: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2689 ... 412     let mut terms = user_prompt
2690 ... 413         .to_ascii_lowercase()
2691 ... 414         .split(|ch: char| !ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric() && ch != '_' && ch != '.')
2692 ... 415         .filter(|term| term.len() >= 3)
2693 ... 416         .filter(|term| {
2694 ... 417             !matches!(
2695 ... 418                 *term,
2696 ... 419                 "the"
2697 ... 420                     | "and"
2698 ... 421                     | "with"
2699 ... 422                     | "from"
2700 ... 423                     | "into"
2701 ... 424                     | "that"
2702 ... 425                     | "this"
2703 ... 426                     | "what"
2704 ... 427                     | "when"
2705 ... 428                     | "where"
2706 ... 429                     | "which"
2707 ... 430                     | "would"
2708 ... 431                     | "could"
2709 ... 432                     | "should"
2710 ... 433                     | "about"
2711 ... 434                     | "your"
2712 ... 435             )
2713 ... 436         })
2714 ... 437         .map(str::to_string)
2715 ... 438         .collect::<Vec<_>>();
2716 ... 439     terms.sort();
2717 ... 440     terms.dedup();
2718 ... 441     terms
2719 ... 442 }

3181 .... 1996 fn format_planner_loop_state_digest(request: &PlannerRequest) -> String {
3182 .... 1997     let remaining_steps = request

3219 .... 2034         }

3223 .... 2038         lines.push("Current notes:".to_string());

3278 .... 2294 fn planner_action_from_envelope(

3375 .... 2391                 query: fallback_planner_query(&request.user_prompt),

3377 .... 2393             },

3379 .... 2395                 .to_string(),
3380 .... 2396         };
3381 .... 2397     }

3386 .... 2402         },

3388 .... 2404             .to_string(),
3389 .... 2405     }

  35  3 ## Implemented Backbone
  36  4

  38  6 - The recursive planner contract lives in [planning.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/domain/ports/planning.rs) and is rendered through typed turn events in [turns.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/domain/model/turns.rs).
  39  7 - The application now routes non-trivial turns through a planner-owned loop in [mod.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/application/mod.rs), with bounded `search`, `read`, `inspect`, `refine`, `branch`, and `stop` actions.
  40  8 - Planner and synthesizer roles are independently configurable through [main.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/main.rs) and [mod.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/application/mod.rs), with the planner adapter wired in [sift_planner.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/sift_planner.rs) and planner action selection implemented in [sift_agent.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/sift_agent.rs).

2644 2546 ... 263 fn discover_linked_documents(agent_path: &Path, contents: &str) -> Vec<PathBuf> {
2645 2547 ... 264     let mut ordered = Vec::new();
2646 2548 ... 265     let mut seen = HashSet::new();
2647 2549 ... 266     for target in extract_markdown_link_targets(contents)
2648 2550 ... 267         .into_iter()
2649 2551 ... 268         .chain(extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents))
2650 2552 ... 269     {
2651 2553 ... 270         let Some(resolved) = resolve_link_target(agent_path, &target) else {
2652 2554 ... 271             continue;
2653 2555 ... 272         };
2654 2556 ... 273         let canonical = canonical_memory_path(&resolved);
2655 2557 ... 274         if seen.insert(canonical) {
2656 2558 ... 275             ordered.push(resolved);
2657 2559 ... 276         }
2658 2560 ... 277     }
2659 2561 ... 278     ordered
2660 2562 ... 279 }
2661 2563 ... 280 
2662 2564 ... 281 fn extract_markdown_link_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2663 2565 ... 282     let mut targets = Vec::new();
2664 2566 ... 283     let mut remainder = contents;
2665 2567 ... 284     while let Some(start) = remainder.find("](") {
2666 2568 ... 285         let candidate = &remainder[start + 2..];
2667 2569 ... 286         let Some(end) = candidate.find(')') else {
2668 2570 ... 287             break;
2669 2571 ... 288         };
2670 2572 ... 289         let target = candidate[..end].trim();
2671 2573 ... 290         if !target.is_empty() {
2672 2574 ... 291             targets.push(target.to_string());
2673 2575 ... 292         }
2674 2576 ... 293         remainder = &candidate[end + 1..];
2675 2577 ... 294     }
2676 2578 ... 295     targets
2677 2579 ... 296 }
2678 2580 ... 297 
2679 2581 ... 298 fn extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2680 2582 ... 299     let mut targets = Vec::new();
2681 2583 ... 300     let mut in_tick = false;
2682 2584 ... 301     let mut current = String::new();
2683 2585 ... 302 
2684 2586 ... 303     for ch in contents.chars() {
2685 2587 ... 304         if ch == '`' {
2686 2588 ... 305             if in_tick {
2687 2589 ... 306                 let trimmed = current.trim();
2688 2590 ... 307                 if looks_like_local_doc_target(trimmed) {
2689 2591 ... 308                     targets.push(trimmed.to_string());
2690 2592 ... 309                 }
2691 2593 ... 310                 current.clear();
2692 2594 ... 311             }
2693 2595 ... 312             in_tick = !in_tick;
2694 2596 ... 313             continue;
2695 2597 ... 314         }
2696 2598 ... 315 
2697 2599 ... 316         if in_tick {
2698 2600 ... 317             current.push(ch);
2699 2601 ... 318         }
2700 2602 ... 319     }
2701 2603 ... 320 
2702 2604 ... 321     targets
2703 2605 ... 322 }

2705 2607 ... 324 fn looks_like_local_doc_target(target: &str) -> bool {
2706 2608 ... 325     target.ends_with(".md") || target.starts_with(".keel/")
2707 2609 ... 326 }

2709 2611 ... 328 fn resolve_link_target(agent_path: &Path, target: &str) -> Option<PathBuf> {
2710 2612 ... 329     if target.starts_with("http://")
2711 2613 ... 330         || target.starts_with("https://")
2712 2614 ... 331         || target.starts_with("mailto:")
2713 2615 ... 332     {
2714 2616 ... 333         return None;
2715 2617 ... 334     }
2716 2618 ... 335 
2717 2619 ... 336     let target = target.split('#').next()?.trim();
2718 2620 ... 337     if target.is_empty() || !looks_like_local_doc_target(target) {
2719 2621 ... 338         return None;
2720 2622 ... 339     }
2721 2623 ... 340 
2722 2624 ... 341     let candidate = if Path::new(target).is_absolute() {
2723 2625 ... 342         PathBuf::from(target)
2724 2626 ... 343     } else {
2725 2627 ... 344         agent_path.parent()?.join(target)
2726 2628 ... 345     };
2727 2629 ... 346 
2728 2630 ... 347     if candidate.is_file() {
2729 2631 ... 348         Some(candidate)
2730 2632 ... 349     } else {
2731 2633 ... 350         None
2732 2634 ... 351     }
2733 2635 ... 352 }

2749 2651 ... 374 fn select_relevant_excerpt(contents: &str, user_prompt: &str) -> (String, usize) {
2750 2652 ... 375     let query_terms = prompt_terms(user_prompt);
2751 2653 ... 376     let lines = contents.lines().collect::<Vec<_>>();
2752 2654 ... 377 
2753 2655 ... 378     let mut excerpt = Vec::new();
2754 2656 ... 379     let mut score = 0;
2755 2657 ... 380     if !query_terms.is_empty() {
2756 2658 ... 381         for (index, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {
2757 2659 ... 382             let normalized = line.to_ascii_lowercase();
2758 2660 ... 383             let matched_terms = query_terms
2759 2661 ... 384                 .iter()
2760 2662 ... 385                 .filter(|term| normalized.contains(term.as_str()))
2761 2663 ... 386                 .count();
2762 2664 ... 387             if matched_terms > 0 {
2763 2665 ... 388                 score += matched_terms;
2764 2666 ... 389                 let start = index.saturating_sub(1);
2765 2667 ... 390                 let end = usize::min(index + 3, lines.len());
2766 2668 ... 391                 excerpt.extend(lines[start..end].iter().copied());
2767 2669 ... 392                 if excerpt.len() >= 8 {
2768 2670 ... 393                     break;
2769 2671 ... 394                 }
2770 2672 ... 395             }
2771 2673 ... 396         }
2772 2674 ... 397     }
2773 2675 ... 398 
2774 2676 ... 399     if excerpt.is_empty() {
2775 2677 ... 400         excerpt.extend(
2776 2678 ... 401             lines
2777 2679 ... 402                 .into_iter()
2778 2680 ... 403                 .filter(|line| !line.trim().is_empty())
2779 2681 ... 404                 .take(8),
2780 2682 ... 405         );
2781 2683 ... 406     }
2782 2684 ... 407 
2783 2685 ... 408     (trim_memory_contents(&excerpt.join("\n")), score)
2784 2686 ... 409 }
2785 2687 ... 410 
2786 2688 ... 411 fn prompt_terms(user_prompt: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2787 2689 ... 412     let mut terms = user_prompt
2788 2690 ... 413         .to_ascii_lowercase()
2789 2691 ... 414         .split(|ch: char| !ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric() && ch != '_' && ch != '.')
2790 2692 ... 415         .filter(|term| term.len() >= 3)
2791 2693 ... 416         .filter(|term| {
2792 2694 ... 417             !matches!(
2793 2695 ... 418                 *term,
2794 2696 ... 419                 "the"
2795 2697 ... 420                     | "and"
2796 2698 ... 421                     | "with"
2797 2699 ... 422                     | "from"
2798 2700 ... 423                     | "into"
2799 2701 ... 424                     | "that"
2800 2702 ... 425                     | "this"
2801 2703 ... 426                     | "what"
2802 2704 ... 427                     | "when"
2803 2705 ... 428                     | "where"
2804 2706 ... 429                     | "which"
2805 2707 ... 430                     | "would"
2806 2708 ... 431                     | "could"
2807 2709 ... 432                     | "should"
2808 2710 ... 433                     | "about"
2809 2711 ... 434                     | "your"
2810 2712 ... 435             )
2811 2713 ... 436         })
2812 2714 ... 437         .map(str::to_string)
2813 2715 ... 438         .collect::<Vec<_>>();
2814 2716 ... 439     terms.sort();
2815 2717 ... 440     terms.dedup();
2816 2718 ... 441     terms
2817 2719 ... 442 }

6101 ... 263 fn discover_linked_documents(agent_path: &Path, contents: &str) -> Vec<PathBuf> {
6102 ... 264     let mut ordered = Vec::new();
6103 ... 265     let mut seen = HashSet::new();
6104 ... 266     for target in extract_markdown_link_targets(contents)
6105 ... 267         .into_iter()
6106 ... 268         .chain(extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents))
6107 ... 269     {
6108 ... 270         let Some(resolved) = resolve_link_target(agent_path, &target) else {
6109 ... 271             continue;
6110 ... 272         };
6111 ... 273         let canonical = canonical_memory_path(&resolved);
6112 ... 274         if seen.insert(canonical) {
6113 ... 275             ordered.push(resolved);
6114 ... 276         }
6115 ... 277     }
6116 ... 278     ordered
6117 ... 279 }
6118 ... 280 
6119 ... 281 fn extract_markdown_link_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
6120 ... 282     let mut targets = Vec::new();
6121 ... 283     let mut remainder = contents;
6122 ... 284     while let Some(start) = remainder.find("](") {
6123 ... 285         let candidate = &remainder[start + 2..];
6124 ... 286         let Some(end) = candidate.find(')') else {
6125 ... 287             break;
6126 ... 288         };
6127 ... 289         let target = candidate[..end].trim();
6128 ... 290         if !target.is_empty() {
6129 ... 291             targets.push(target.to_string());
6130 ... 292         }
6131 ... 293         remainder = &candidate[end + 1..];
6132 ... 294     }
6133 ... 295     targets
6134 ... 296 }
6135 ... 297 
6136 ... 298 fn extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
6137 ... 299     let mut targets = Vec::new();
6138 ... 300     let mut in_tick = false;
6139 ... 301     let mut current = String::new();
6140 ... 302 
6141 ... 303     for ch in contents.chars() {
6142 ... 304         if ch == '`' {
6143 ... 305             if in_tick {
6144 ... 306                 let trimmed = current.trim();
6145 ... 307                 if looks_like_local_doc_target(trimmed) {
6146 ... 308                     targets.push(trimmed.to_string());
6147 ... 309                 }
6148 ... 310                 current.clear();
6149 ... 311             }
6150 ... 312             in_tick = !in_tick;
6151 ... 313             continue;
6152 ... 314         }
6153 ... 315 
6154 ... 316         if in_tick {
6155 ... 317             current.push(ch);
6156 ... 318         }
6157 ... 319     }
6158 ... 320 
6159 ... 321     targets
6160 ... 322 }
6161 ... 323 
6162 ... 324 fn looks_like_local_doc_target(target: &str) -> bool {
6163 ... 325     target.ends_with(".md") || target.starts_with(".keel/")
6164 ... 326 }
6165 ... 327 
6166 ... 328 fn resolve_link_target(agent_path: &Path, target: &str) -> Option<PathBuf> {
6167 ... 329     if target.starts_with("http://")
6168 ... 330         || target.starts_with("https://")
6169 ... 331         || target.starts_with("mailto:")
6170 ... 332     {
6171 ... 333         return None;
6172 ... 334     }
6173 ... 335 
6174 ... 336     let target = target.split('#').next()?.trim();
6175 ... 337     if target.is_empty() || !looks_like_local_doc_target(target) {
6176 ... 338         return None;
6177 ... 339     }
6178 ... 340 
6179 ... 341     let candidate = if Path::new(target).is_absolute() {
6180 ... 342         PathBuf::from(target)
6181 ... 343     } else {
6182 ... 344         agent_path.parent()?.join(target)
6183 ... 345     };
6184 ... 346 
6185 ... 347     if candidate.is_file() {
6186 ... 348         Some(candidate)
6187 ... 349     } else {
6188 ... 350         None
6189 ... 351     }
6190 ... 352 }

6206 ... 374 fn select_relevant_excerpt(contents: &str, user_prompt: &str) -> (String, usize) {
6207 ... 375     let query_terms = prompt_terms(user_prompt);
6208 ... 376     let lines = contents.lines().collect::<Vec<_>>();
6209 ... 377 
6210 ... 378     let mut excerpt = Vec::new();
6211 ... 379     let mut score = 0;
6212 ... 380     if !query_terms.is_empty() {
6213 ... 381         for (index, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {
6214 ... 382             let normalized = line.to_ascii_lowercase();
6215 ... 383             let matched_terms = query_terms
6216 ... 384                 .iter()
6217 ... 385                 .filter(|term| normalized.contains(term.as_str()))
6218 ... 386                 .count();
6219 ... 387             if matched_terms > 0 {
6220 ... 388                 score += matched_terms;
6221 ... 389                 let start = index.saturating_sub(1);
6222 ... 390                 let end = usize::min(index + 3, lines.len());
6223 ... 391                 excerpt.extend(lines[start..end].iter().copied());
6224 ... 392                 if excerpt.len() >= 8 {
6225 ... 393                     break;
6226 ... 394                 }
6227 ... 395             }
6228 ... 396         }
6229 ... 397     }
6230 ... 398 
6231 ... 399     if excerpt.is_empty() {
6232 ... 400         excerpt.extend(
6233 ... 401             lines
6234 ... 402                 .into_iter()
6235 ... 403                 .filter(|line| !line.trim().is_empty())
6236 ... 404                 .take(8),
6237 ... 405         );
6238 ... 406     }
6239 ... 407 
6240 ... 408     (trim_memory_contents(&excerpt.join("\n")), score)
6241 ... 409 }
6242 ... 410 
6243 ... 411 fn prompt_terms(user_prompt: &str) -> Vec<String> {
6244 ... 412     let mut terms = user_prompt
6245 ... 413         .to_ascii_lowercase()
6246 ... 414         .split(|ch: char| !ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric() && ch != '_' && ch != '.')
6247 ... 415         .filter(|term| term.len() >= 3)
6248 ... 416         .filter(|term| {
6249 ... 417             !matches!(
6250 ... 418                 *term,
6251 ... 419                 "the"
6252 ... 420                     | "and"
6253 ... 421                     | "with"
6254 ... 422                     | "from"
6255 ... 423                     | "into"
6256 ... 424                     | "that"
6257 ... 425                     | "this"
6258 ... 426                     | "what"
6259 ... 427                     | "when"
6260 ... 428                     | "where"
6261 ... 429                     | "which"
6262 ... 430                     | "would"
6263 ... 431                     | "could"
6264 ... 432                     | "should"
6265 ... 433                     | "about"
6266 ... 434                     | "your"
6267 ... 435             )
6268 ... 436         })
6269 ... 437         .map(str::to_string)
6270 ... 438         .collect::<Vec<_>>();
6271 ... 439     terms.sort();
6272 ... 440     terms.dedup();
6273 ... 441     terms
6274 ... 442 }

6736 .... 1996 fn format_planner_loop_state_digest(request: &PlannerRequest) -> String {
6737 .... 1997     let remaining_steps = request
6738 .... 1998         .budget
6739 .... 1999         .max_steps
6740 .... 2000         .saturating_sub(request.loop_state.steps.len());
6741 .... 2001     let mut lines = vec![format!(
6742 .... 2002         "Budget remaining: steps={}, evidence_limit={}, pending_branches={}",
6743 .... 2003         remaining_steps,
6744 .... 2004         request.budget.max_evidence_items,
6745 .... 2005         request.loop_state.pending_branches.len()
6746 .... 2006     )];
6747 .... 2007 
6748 .... 2008     if request.loop_state.steps.is_empty() {
6749 .... 2009         lines.push("No planner steps have executed yet.".to_string());
6750 .... 2010     } else {
6751 .... 2011         for step in request.loop_state.steps.iter().rev().take(4).rev() {
6752 .... 2012             lines.push(format!(
6753 .... 2013                 "- step {}: {} -> {}",
6754 .... 2014                 step.sequence,
6755 .... 2015                 step.action.summary(),
6756 .... 2016                 trim_for_context(&step.outcome, 180)
6757 .... 2017             ));
6758 .... 2018         }
6759 .... 2019     }
6760 .... 2020 
6761 .... 2021     if !request.loop_state.evidence_items.is_empty() {
6762 .... 2022         lines.push("Current evidence:".to_string());
6763 .... 2023         for item in request
6764 .... 2024             .loop_state
6765 .... 2025             .evidence_items
6766 .... 2026             .iter()
6767 .... 2027             .take(request.budget.max_evidence_items.min(4))
6768 .... 2028         {
6769 .... 2029             lines.push(format!(
6770 .... 2030                 "- {}: {}",
6771 .... 2031                 item.source,
6772 .... 2032                 trim_for_context(&item.snippet, 180)
6773 .... 2033             ));
6774 .... 2034         }
6775 .... 2035     }
6776 .... 2036 
6777 .... 2037     if !request.loop_state.notes.is_empty() {
6778 .... 2038         lines.push("Current notes:".to_string());
6779 .... 2039         for note in request.loop_state.notes.iter().take(3) {
6780 .... 2040             lines.push(format!("- {}", trim_for_context(note, 180)));
6781 .... 2041         }
6782 .... 2042     }
6783 .... 2043 
6784 .... 2044     if !request.loop_state.pending_branches.is_empty() {
6785 .... 2045         lines.push(format!(
6786 .... 2046             "Pending branches: {}",
6787 .... 2047             request.loop_state.pending_branches.join(" | ")
6788 .... 2048         ));
6789 .... 2049     }
6790 .... 2050

...  571         &self,

...  573         context: PlannerLoopContext,
...  574         event_sink: Arc<dyn TurnEventSink>,
...  575     ) -> Result<Option<EvidenceBundle>> {
...  576         let budget = PlannerBudget::default();
...  577         let mut loop_state = PlannerLoopState::default();
...  578         let mut used_workspace_resources = false;

...  580         let gatherer_provider = context
...  581             .prepared
...  582             .gatherer

...  595             .with_loop_state(loop_state.clone());
...  596             let decision = context.planner_engine.select_next_action(&request).await?;
...  597             event_sink.emit(TurnEvent::PlannerActionSelected {
...  598                 sequence,
...  599                 action: decision.action.summary(),
...  600                 rationale: decision.rationale.clone(),
...  601             });
...  602 
...  603             let outcome = match &decision.action {
...  604                 PlannerAction::Search { query, intent } => {
...  605                     if let Some(gatherer) = context.gatherer.as_ref() {
...  606                         event_sink.emit(TurnEvent::GathererCapability {
...  607                             provider: gatherer_provider.clone(),
...  608                             capability: format_gatherer_capability(&gatherer.capability()),
...  609                         });

...  615                                     intent
...  616                                         .clone()
...  617                                         .unwrap_or_else(|| "planner-search".to_string()),
...  618                                     EvidenceBudget::default(),

...  621                                 .with_prior_context(
...  622                                     build_planner_prior_context(

...  629                                     Ok(result) => {

...  633                                                 provider: gatherer_provider.clone(),

...  649                                                 });
...  650                                             }

...  654                                                 budget.max_evidence_items,
...  655                                             );
...  656                                             loop_state.notes.extend(bundle.warnings.clone());
...  657                                             used_workspace_resources = true;
...  658                                             bundle.summary.clone()
...  659                                         } else {

...  661                                         }
...  662                                     }

... 262 
... 263 fn discover_linked_documents(agent_path: &Path, contents: &str) -> Vec<PathBuf> {
... 264     let mut ordered = Vec::new();
... 265     let mut seen = HashSet::new();
... 266     for target in extract_markdown_link_targets(contents)
... 267         .into_iter()
... 268         .chain(extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents))
... 269     {
... 270         let Some(resolved) = resolve_link_target(agent_path, &target) else {
... 271             continue;
... 272         };
... 273         let canonical = canonical_memory_path(&resolved);
... 274         if seen.insert(canonical) {
... 275             ordered.push(resolved);
... 276         }
... 277     }
... 278     ordered
... 279 }
... 280 
... 281 fn extract_markdown_link_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
... 282     let mut targets = Vec::new();
... 283     let mut remainder = contents;
... 284     while let Some(start) = remainder.find("](") {
... 285         let candidate = &remainder[start + 2..];
... 286         let Some(end) = candidate.find(')') else {
... 287             break;
... 288         };
... 289         let target = candidate[..end].trim();
... 290         if !target.is_empty() {
... 291             targets.push(target.to_string());
... 292         }
... 293         remainder = &candidate[end + 1..];
... 294     }
... 295     targets
... 296 }
... 297 
... 298 fn extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
... 299     let mut targets = Vec::new();
... 300     let mut in_tick = false;
... 301     let mut current = String::new();
... 302 
... 303     for ch in contents.chars() {
... 304         if ch == '`' {
... 305             if in_tick {
... 306                 let trimmed = current.trim();
... 307                 if looks_like_local_doc_target(trimmed) {
... 308                     targets.push(trimmed.to_string());
... 309                 }
... 310                 current.clear();
... 311             }
... 312             in_tick = !in_tick;
... 313             continue;
... 314         }
... 315 
... 316         if in_tick {
... 317             current.push(ch);
... 318         }
... 319     }
... 320 
... 321     targets
... 322 }
... 323 
... 324 fn looks_like_local_doc_target(target: &str) -> bool {
... 325     target.ends_with(".md") || target.starts_with(".keel/")
... 326 }
... 327 
... 328 fn resolve_link_target(agent_path: &Path, target: &str) -> Option<PathBuf> {
... 329     if target.starts_with("http://")
... 330         || target.starts_with("https://")
... 331         || target.starts_with("mailto:")
... 332     {
... 333         return None;
... 334     }
... 335 
... 336     let target = target.split('#').next()?.trim();
... 337     if target.is_empty() || !looks_like_local_doc_target(target) {
... 338         return None;
... 339     }
... 340 
... 341     let candidate = if Path::new(target).is_absolute() {
... 342         PathBuf::from(target)
... 343     } else {
... 344         agent_path.parent()?.join(target)
... 345     };
... 346 
... 347     if candidate.is_file() {
... 348         Some(candidate)
... 349     } else {
... 350         None
... 351     }
... 352 }

160 354 fn trim_memory_contents(contents: &str) -> String {
161 355     if contents.chars().count() <= MAX_MEMORY_FILE_CHARS {

src/infrastructure/adapters/agent_memory.rs --- 8/9 --- Rust
170 364     trimmed
171 365 }
... 366 
... 367 fn display_path(workspace_root: &Path, path: &Path) -> String {
... 368     path.strip_prefix(workspace_root)
... 369         .unwrap_or(path)
... 370         .display()
... 371         .to_string()
... 372 }
... 373 
... 374 fn select_relevant_excerpt(contents: &str, user_prompt: &str) -> (String, usize) {
... 375     let query_terms = prompt_terms(user_prompt);
... 376     let lines = contents.lines().collect::<Vec<_>>();
... 377 
... 378     let mut excerpt = Vec::new();
... 379     let mut score = 0;
... 380     if !query_terms.is_empty() {
... 381         for (index, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {
... 382             let normalized = line.to_ascii_lowercase();
... 383             let matched_terms = query_terms
... 384                 .iter()
... 385                 .filter(|term| normalized.contains(term.as_str()))
... 386                 .count();
... 387             if matched_terms > 0 {
... 388                 score += matched_terms;
... 389                 let start = index.saturating_sub(1);
... 390                 let end = usize::min(index + 3, lines.len());
... 391                 excerpt.extend(lines[start..end].iter().copied());
... 392                 if excerpt.len() >= 8 {
... 393                     break;
... 394                 }
... 395             }
... 396         }
... 397     }
... 398 
... 399     if excerpt.is_empty() {
... 400         excerpt.extend(
... 401             lines
... 402                 .into_iter()
... 403                 .filter(|line| !line.trim().is_empty())
... 404                 .take(8),
... 405         );
... 406     }
... 407 
... 408     (trim_memory_contents(&excerpt.join("\n")), score)
... 409 }
... 410 
... 411 fn prompt_terms(user_prompt: &str) -> Vec<String> {
... 412     let mut terms = user_prompt
... 413         .to_ascii_lowercase()
... 414         .split(|ch: char| !ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric() && ch != '_' && ch != '.')
... 415         .filter(|term| term.len() >= 3)
... 416         .filter(|term| {
... 417             !matches!(
... 418                 *term,
... 419                 "the"
... 420                     | "and"
... 421                     | "with"
... 422                     | "from"
... 423                     | "into"
... 424                     | "that"
... 425                     | "this"
... 426                     | "what"
... 427                     | "when"
... 428                     | "where"
... 429                     | "which"
... 430                     | "would"
... 431                     | "could"
... 432                     | "should"
... 433                     | "about"
... 434                     | "your"
... 435             )
... 436         })
... 437         .map(str::to_string)
... 438         .collect::<Vec<_>>();
... 439     terms.sort();
... 440     terms.dedup();
... 441     terms
... 442 }

 ...  829     ) -> Result<RecursivePlannerDecision> {
 ...  830         let mut conversation = self.conversation_factory.start_conversation()?;
 ...  831         let mut reply = self.send_to_model(
 ...  832             conversation.as_mut(),
 ...  833             &build_planner_action_prompt(&PlannerPrompt {
 ...  834                 workspace_root: &request.workspace_root,
 ...  835                 user_prompt: &request.user_prompt,
 ...  836                 interpretation: &request.interpretation,
 ...  837                 request,
 ...  838             }),
 ...  839         )?;
 ...  840 
 ...  841         if is_blank_model_reply(&reply) || parse_planner_action(&reply)?.is_none() {
 ...  842             self.log_retry_reason(
 ...  843                 "planner-retry",
 ...  844                 &reply,
 ...  845                 "missing or invalid planner action response",
 ...  846             );
 ...  847             reply =
 ...  848                 self.send_to_model(conversation.as_mut(), &build_planner_retry_prompt(request))?;
 ...  849         }
 ...  850 
 ...  851         if let Some(decision) = parse_planner_action(&reply)? {
 ...  852             return Ok(decision);
 ...  853         }
 ...  854 
 ...  855         self.log_retry_reason(
 ...  856             "planner-fallback",
 ...  857             &reply,
 ...  858             "falling back to bounded heuristic planner action",
 ...  859         );
 ...  860         Ok(fallback_planner_action(request))
 ...  861     }

.... 1996 fn format_planner_loop_state_digest(request: &PlannerRequest) -> String {
.... 1997     let remaining_steps = request
.... 1998         .budget
.... 1999         .max_steps
.... 2000         .saturating_sub(request.loop_state.steps.len());
.... 2001     let mut lines = vec![format!(
.... 2002         "Budget remaining: steps={}, evidence_limit={}, pending_branches={}",
.... 2003         remaining_steps,
.... 2004         request.budget.max_evidence_items,
.... 2005         request.loop_state.pending_branches.len()
.... 2006     )];
.... 2007 
.... 2008     if request.loop_state.steps.is_empty() {
.... 2009         lines.push("No planner steps have executed yet.".to_string());
.... 2010     } else {
.... 2011         for step in request.loop_state.steps.iter().rev().take(4).rev() {
.... 2012             lines.push(format!(
.... 2013                 "- step {}: {} -> {}",
.... 2014                 step.sequence,
.... 2015                 step.action.summary(),
.... 2016                 trim_for_context(&step.outcome, 180)
.... 2017             ));
.... 2018         }
.... 2019     }
.... 2020 
.... 2021     if !request.loop_state.evidence_items.is_empty() {
.... 2022         lines.push("Current evidence:".to_string());
.... 2023         for item in request
.... 2024             .loop_state
.... 2025             .evidence_items
.... 2026             .iter()
.... 2027             .take(request.budget.max_evidence_items.min(4))
.... 2028         {
.... 2029             lines.push(format!(
.... 2030                 "- {}: {}",
.... 2031                 item.source,
.... 2032                 trim_for_context(&item.snippet, 180)
.... 2033             ));
.... 2034         }
.... 2035     }
.... 2036 
.... 2037     if !request.loop_state.notes.is_empty() {
.... 2038         lines.push("Current notes:".to_string());
.... 2039         for note in request.loop_state.notes.iter().take(3) {
.... 2040             lines.push(format!("- {}", trim_for_context(note, 180)));
.... 2041         }
.... 2042     }
.... 2043 
.... 2044     if !request.loop_state.pending_branches.is_empty() {
.... 2045         lines.push(format!(
.... 2046             "Pending branches: {}",
.... 2047             request.loop_state.pending_branches.join(" | ")
.... 2048         ));
.... 2049     }
.... 2050 
.... 2051     lines.join("\n")
.... 2052 }

.... 2282 fn parse_planner_action(response: &str) -> Result<Option<RecursivePlannerDecision>> {
.... 2283     let trimmed = response.trim();
.... 2284     let Some(json) = extract_json_payload(trimmed) else {
.... 2285         return Ok(None);
.... 2286     };

.... 2288         return Ok(None);
.... 2289     };
.... 2290 
.... 2291     Ok(Some(planner_action_from_envelope(action)?))
.... 2292 }
.... 2293 
.... 2294 fn planner_action_from_envelope(
.... 2295     envelope: PlannerActionEnvelope,
.... 2296 ) -> Result<RecursivePlannerDecision> {
.... 2297     let decision = match envelope {
.... 2298         PlannerActionEnvelope::Search {
.... 2299             query,
.... 2300             intent,
.... 2301             rationale,
.... 2302         } => RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2303             action: PlannerAction::Search {
.... 2304                 query: required_planner_field("query", query)?,
.... 2305                 intent: intent.and_then(|value| {
.... 2306                     let trimmed = value.trim();
.... 2307                     (!trimmed.is_empty()).then(|| trimmed.to_string())
.... 2308                 }),
.... 2309             },
.... 2310             rationale: required_planner_field("rationale", rationale)?,
.... 2311         },
.... 2312         PlannerActionEnvelope::Read { path, rationale } => RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2313             action: PlannerAction::Read {
.... 2314                 path: required_planner_field("path", path)?,
.... 2315             },
.... 2316             rationale: required_planner_field("rationale", rationale)?,
.... 2317         },
.... 2318         PlannerActionEnvelope::Inspect { command, rationale } => RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2319             action: PlannerAction::Inspect {
.... 2320                 command: required_planner_field("command", command)?,
.... 2321             },
.... 2322             rationale: required_planner_field("rationale", rationale)?,
.... 2323         },
.... 2324         PlannerActionEnvelope::Refine { query, rationale } => {
.... 2325             let rationale_text = rationale
.... 2326                 .as_deref()
.... 2327                 .map(str::trim)
.... 2328                 .filter(|value| !value.is_empty())
.... 2329                 .map(str::to_string);
.... 2330             RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2331                 action: PlannerAction::Refine {
.... 2332                     query: required_planner_field("query", query)?,
.... 2333                     rationale: rationale_text.clone(),
.... 2334                 },
.... 2335                 rationale: rationale_text.unwrap_or_else(|| "refine the investigation".to_string()),
.... 2336             }
.... 2337         }
.... 2338         PlannerActionEnvelope::Branch {
.... 2339             branches,
.... 2340             rationale,
.... 2341         } => {
.... 2342             let branches = branches
.... 2343                 .into_iter()
.... 2344                 .map(|branch| branch.trim().to_string())
.... 2345                 .filter(|branch| !branch.is_empty())
.... 2346                 .collect::<Vec<_>>();
.... 2347             if branches.is_empty() {
.... 2348                 bail!("planner branch action must include at least one branch");
.... 2349             }
.... 2350             RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2351                 action: PlannerAction::Branch {
.... 2352                     branches,
.... 2353                     rationale: rationale.clone(),
.... 2354                 },
.... 2355                 rationale: rationale.unwrap_or_else(|| "branch the investigation".to_string()),
.... 2356             }
.... 2357         }
.... 2358         PlannerActionEnvelope::Stop { reason, rationale } => RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2359             action: PlannerAction::Stop {
.... 2360                 reason: required_planner_field("reason", reason)?,
.... 2361             },
.... 2362             rationale: rationale.unwrap_or_else(|| "stop planning".to_string()),
.... 2363         },
.... 2364     };
.... 2365 
.... 2366     Ok(decision)
.... 2367 }

.... 2369 fn required_planner_field(name: &str, value: String) -> Result<String> {
.... 2370     let trimmed = value.trim();
.... 2371     if trimmed.is_empty() {
.... 2372         bail!("planner field `{name}` must not be empty");
.... 2373     }
.... 2374     Ok(trimmed.to_string())

.... 2377 fn fallback_planner_action(request: &PlannerRequest) -> RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2378     if let Some(branch) = request.loop_state.pending_branches.first() {
.... 2379         return RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2380             action: PlannerAction::Search {
.... 2381                 query: branch.clone(),
.... 2382                 intent: Some("queued planner branch".to_string()),
.... 2383             },
.... 2384             rationale: "continue with the oldest queued branch".to_string(),
.... 2385         };
.... 2386     }
.... 2387 
.... 2388     if request.loop_state.steps.is_empty() && request.loop_state.evidence_items.is_empty() {
.... 2389         return RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2390             action: PlannerAction::Search {
.... 2391                 query: fallback_planner_query(&request.user_prompt),
.... 2392                 intent: Some("initial planner fallback".to_string()),
.... 2393             },
.... 2394             rationale: "start with a bounded workspace search when the planner reply is invalid"
.... 2395                 .to_string(),

.... 2397     }
.... 2398 
.... 2399     RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2400         action: PlannerAction::Stop {
.... 2401             reason: "planner fallback stop".to_string(),
.... 2402         },
.... 2403         rationale: "stop after invalid planner replies once some loop state already exists"
.... 2404             .to_string(),
.... 2405     }
.... 2406 }
